1. # SÎYA EVÎNÊ
1. # THE SHADOW OF LOVE

2. Roman by Mehmed Uzun.
2. Roman by Mehmed Uzun.

3. ## LÎ SER RÎYA KOÇA DAWÎN
3. ## ON THE ROAD OF THE FINAL MIGRATION

4. 1976, payiz.
4. 1976, autumn.

5. Koç.
5. Migration.
6. Bi dû payiza jiyanê re koça dawîn.
6. Following the autumn of life, the final migration.
7. Bêdeng, bêpejn.
7. Silent, without sound.
8. Wext naxuye, cih û war naxuyin.
8. Time is not seen, place and dwelling are not seen.
9. Yan jî ew dixuyin, lê tevlihev.
9. Or else they appear, but mixed up.
10. Hem ev der û hem ew der.
10. Both this place and that place.
11. Hem niha, hem do û pêr.
11. Both now, both yesterday and the day before yesterday.
12. Hem nêzîk, hem dûr.
12. Both near, both far.
13. Koçeke rengîn, xweş, bêdawî, bê lez û bez, bê teşqele, bê westan û xwîdan.
13. A migration colorful, pleasant, endless, without haste and speed, without trouble, without fatigue and sweat.
14. Koçeke ji hesûdî, pexîlî, dijminahî, xirabî, kiretî, fetbazî, xwînrêjî bi dûr.
14. A migration far from envy, jealousy, enmity, badness, ugliness, intrigue, bloodshed.
15. Koçeke xweş li gor daxwaza dilên xweş.
15. A migration pleasant according to the desire of pleasant hearts.
16. Koçeke mirazkirî.
16. A wished-for migration.
17. Memduh Selîm beg.
17. Memduh Selim Beg.
18. Kalemêrê hêja Memduh Selîm begê Wanî koç dike.
18. The worthy old man Memduh Selim Beg of Wan is migrating.
19. Li ser textê xwe dirêjbûyî.
19. Stretched out on his bed.
20. Çav vekirî.
20. Eyes open.
21. Rûken.
21. Smiling.
22. Lê kerr û lal.
22. But deaf and mute.
23. Çavên wî yên stûr ewçend vekirî ne ku ew weke du lûlûyên stûr dixuyin.
23. His large eyes are so open that they look like two large pearls.
24. Bîbûkên reş yên çavên wî, bê hereket, li jor dinihêrin.
24. The black pupils of his eyes, without movement, look upward.
25. Weke xewnekê.
25. Like a dream.
26. Rûyekî aram.
26. A calm face.
27. Qermîçekên salan lê.
27. Wrinkles of years on it.
28. Porekî spî û nîvweşiyayî.
28. Hair white and half-shed.
29. Lêvên guvaştî.
29. Pressed lips.
30. Çermê vekişiyayî yê rû.
30. The stretched skin of the face.
31. Stûyê qermiçî.
31. Wrinkled neck.
32. Merivekî kal, bi qasî mistekê.
32. An old man, as much as a fist.
33. «Memduh beg, Memduh beg...»
33. «Memduh Beg, Memduh Beg...»
34. Ew nabihîse.
34. He does not hear.
35. Ew tu tişt nabihîse êdî, bi rê ketiye, koç dike.
35. He hears nothing anymore, has set off, is migrating.
36. Li dorê, jina wî Wildan xanim û çend xort.
36. Around, his wife Wildan Xanim and a few youths.

37. Li ber serî jî pise pisa pîrejinekê.
37. At the head also is the whispering of an old woman.
38. Pîrejin Qur'an dixwîne.
38. The old woman is reading the Qur'an.
39. Çar aliyên dîwêr bi refên kitêban ve tijî.
39. Four sides of the wall are full of shelves of books.
40. Kitêb, kovar, rojname û kaxiz.
40. Books, magazines, newspapers, and papers.
41. Li ser refan çend lewheyên zerbûyî; du sûret û du bergeh.
41. On the shelves are several yellowed frames; two portraits and two landscapes.
42. Di navenda odê de jî ew; Memduh Selîm beg.
42. In the center of the room also is he; Memduh Selim Beg.
43. Ew di nav xewnekê de koç dike.
43. He is migrating inside a dream.
44. Ew bi xwe, li ser cihê xwe dirêj bûye û ber bi cihekî nare.
44. He himself has stretched out on his bed and is not going toward any place.
45. Lê, tişt, cih û wextên têkel bi ser wî re tên.
45. But, mixed things, places, and times are coming over him.
46. Ew di nav tişt, cih û wextên têkel de koç dike.
46. He is migrating inside mixed things, places, and times.
47. Rabirdû û niha ketine nav hev; deşt, çiya, zozan, newal, daristan bi hev re bûne yek; derya û asman gihîştine hevûdu, meriv, heywan, lawir û celeb bi celeb mehlûqat reng û rûçik diguherînin, dikevin dewsa hev.
47. The past and present have fallen into each other; plains, mountains, summer-pastures, valleys, forests have become one together; the sea and sky have reached each other, people, beasts, birds, and type by type of creatures change color and appearance, falling into each other's places.
48. Lê tirs tune, sarî û germî tune, heyecan tune, hîs û pejn tune.
48. But fear is not, cold and heat are not, excitement is not, feeling and sense are not.
49. Deng jê dernakeve, nefes lê naçike, qîrîn jê ranabe, pîqîn pê nakeve.
49. Voice does not come out of him, breath does not choke in him, scream does not rise from him, shriek does not catch him.
50. Ew der e.
50. That place is.
51. Devereke rengîn.
51. A colorful region.
52. Heye ku daristaneke xweş, yan jî zozaneke hûnik e.
52. It may be a pleasant forest, or else a cool summer-pasture.
53. Memduh Selîm beg li ser deverê rengîn.
53. Memduh Selim Beg is on the colorful region.
54. Der û dorên wî tijî kew û kevok.
54. His surroundings are full of partridges and pigeons.
55. Ew di nav kew û kevokan de li jêr, li deverê rengîn dinihêre.
55. Inside the partridges and pigeons, he looks down at the colorful region.
56. Du kewên spî, li her du aliyên wî, difirin.
56. Two white partridges, on both his sides, are flying.
57. Kew her gav nêzîkî wî ne.
57. The partridges are close to him at every step.
58. Reng, bask, perwaz, nikul û çavên kewan baş dixuyin.
58. The color, wings, flight, beak, and eyes of the partridges appear well.
59. Çavên wan weke dilopên avê zelal û xweş.
59. Their eyes are clear and pleasant like drops of water.
60. Ew bêdeng difirin.
60. They fly silently.
61. Memduh Selîm beg, carina li kewa kêleka rastê, carina jî li ya çepê dinihêre.
61. Memduh Selim Beg looks sometimes at the partridge of the right side, sometimes also at that of the left.
62. Kewên din jî ref bi ref difirin.
62. The other partridges also fly flock by flock.
63. Reng û stûrahiyên wan têkel in.
63. Their colors and thicknesses are mixed.
64. Ew difirin.
64. They fly.
65. Memduh Selîm beg jî hem difire, hem nafire; hem dimeşe, hem nameşe; hem li jêr, hem li jor e.
65. Memduh Selim Beg also both flies and does not fly; both walks and does not walk; is both below and above.
66. Lê belê, tiştê herî balkêş bêdengî ye.
66. But indeed, the most interesting thing is silence.
67. Hawirdor bi bêdengiyê hatiye vegirtin.
67. The surroundings have been enveloped in silence.
68. Perda bêdengiyê bi ser her tiştî re hatiye kişandin.
68. The veil of silence has been pulled over everything.
69. «Memduh beg, binihêre, xortê hêja Gurgîn jî hat...»
69. «Memduh Beg, look, the worthy youth Gurgin also came...»

70. Wildan xanim, bi hêdîka, li ber guhê wî dipeyive û destê wî yê rastê dixe nav lepê xwe û dest mist dide.
70. Wildan Xanim, softly, speaks by his ear and puts his right hand inside her palm and strokes the hand.
71. Deng nagihên wî.
71. Voices do not reach him.
72. Perda bêdengiyê nahêle ku deng xwe biguhezînin wî.
72. The veil of silence does not let voices convey themselves to him.
73. Memduh Selîm beg hem li nik wan e, hem jî na; hem dijî, hem jî najî; hem li vê dinê ye, hem jî na.
73. Memduh Selim Beg is both near them and also not; both lives and also does not live; is both in this world and also not.
74. Xort cot bi cot tên û li ber serê wî rûdinin.
74. The youths come pair by pair and sit at his head-side.
75. Wildan xanim, di nav kincên xwe yên reş de, her li ser serê wî ye.
75. Wildan Xanim, in her black clothes, is always over his head.
76. Wan, xort û Wildan xanim, hêvî heye ku Memduh Selîm beg dev ji koça dilsoj berde û li wan vegere.
76. They, the youths and Wildan Xanim, have hope that Memduh Selim Beg will abandon the heartbreaking migration and return to them.
77. «Apê Memduh, bavê min, mala xalanên min û Kurdên bajarê Qamişloyê silav li te dikin û ji Xwedê şîfa dixwazin...»
77. «Uncle Memduh, my father, my maternal uncles' house, and the Kurds of the city of Qamishlo send you greetings and wish you healing from God...»
78. Memduh Selîm beg di koça xwe de, niha jî, bajarekî dibîne.
78. Memduh Selim Beg in his migration, now also, sees a city.
79. Ji dûr ve.
79. From afar.
80. Na, carina ji dûr, carina ji nêzîk ve.
80. No, sometimes from afar, sometimes from near.
81. Lê ew tu carî nakeve nav bajêr.
81. But he never enters into the city.
82. Dora bajêr bi sûran hatiye rapêçandin.
82. The city's surroundings have been wrapped with ramparts.
83. Çend bircên fireh li ser sûran dixuyin.
83. Several wide towers appear on the ramparts.
84. Sûr û bircên spehî û stûr.
84. Beautiful and thick ramparts and towers.
85. Ji kevirên reş û stûr.
85. From black and thick stones.
86. Hin aliyên sûran hilweşiyayî ne.
86. Some sides of the ramparts are ruined.
87. Hin qulên mezin jî di bedenên wan de vebûne.
87. Some large holes also have opened in their bodies.
88. Bi dû sûr û bircan re, banên xaniyên bajêr dixuyin.
88. Following the ramparts and towers, the roofs of the city's houses appear.
89. Çend avahiyên mezin ber bi jor, ber bi asmên hildikişin.
89. Several large buildings climb upward, toward the sky.
90. Piraniya xaniyan bi kevirên reş hatine lêkirin.
90. Most of the houses have been built with black stones.
91. Hin jî bi kevirên spî.
91. Some also with white stones.
92. Li dora sûran jî hêşînahî û av dixuyin.
92. Around the ramparts also greenery and water appear.
93. Lê, tu tiştê jîndar naxuye.
93. But no living thing appears.
94. Ne meriv, ne teyr, ne masî, ne heywan û ne jî mehlûqatên din.
94. Not a person, not a bird, not a fish, not a beast, and not other creatures either.
95. Bajar weke hêlekanekê der e û tê, dûr û nêz dibe.
95. The city like a swing goes out and comes, becomes far and near.
96. Bajar di dewsa xwe de diheze.
96. The city shakes in its place.
97. Bajar carina mezin, carina biçûk dibe.
97. The city sometimes becomes large, sometimes small.
98. Ew avahiyên mezin û dirêj carina pir, carina jî kêm dibin.
98. Those large and tall buildings sometimes become many, sometimes also few.
99. Hêşînahî û av carina ji sûr û bircan vediqetin û bi dûr dikevin û carina jî tên pê re yek dibin.
99. The greenery and water sometimes separate from the ramparts and towers and go far, and sometimes come to become one with them.
100. Memduh Selîm beg hewl dide ku bajêr binase, bizanibe ka ew kîjan bajar e, li kû ye.
100. Memduh Selim Beg tries to recognize the city, to know which city it is, where it is.
101. Lê nabe.
101. But it does not happen.
102. Bajar jê bi dûr e.
102. The city is far from him.

103. Bi tenê bajarekî carina biçûk, carina mezin, lê bi sûr û birc.
103. Only a city, sometimes small, sometimes large, but with ramparts and towers.
104. «Apê Memduh, me kitêbên te, yek bi yek, ji nû ve, rêz kirin.
104. «Uncle Memduh, we arranged your books, one by one, anew.
105. Binihêre, kitêbên bi zimanê kurdî li ser van refan in.
105. Look, the books in the Kurdish language are on these shelves.
106. Hemû ev alî jî ji bo kitêbên bi zimanê tirkî ye.
106. All this side also is for books in the Turkish language.
107. Ev çar refên aliyê çepê jî ji bo kitêbên fransizî ne.
107. These four shelves of the left side also are for French books.
108. Refên mayî jî yên kitêbên bi zimanên erebî, farisî, îngilizî û rûsî ne...
108. The remaining shelves also are of books in the Arabic, Persian, English, and Russian languages...
109. Me rojname, kovar û tiştên din jî xistin van sandûqan.
109. We put the newspapers, magazines, and other things also into these boxes.
110. Helbet, bi dûzan.»
110. Of course, with order.»
111. Memduh Selîm beg, hosteyê xewnan, di nav xewneke rengîn de ye.
111. Memduh Selim Beg, the master of dreams, is inside a colorful dream.
112. Koça wî di eynî wext de xewnek e jî.
112. His migration at the same time is a dream also.
113. Lê ev xewnên niha ne asayî ne, ew ne weke xewnên berê ne.
113. But these dreams of now are not ordinary; they are not like the dreams of before.
114. Berê xewnên xoftijî, xewnên malkambax şevên wî dikirin jahr.
114. Before, terrifying dreams, disastrous dreams made his nights poison.
115. Ew di nav xwîdanê de dima û bi qîrîn hişyar dibû.
115. He remained in sweat and woke up with a scream.
116. Carina jî xewnên xweş bi ser wî re dihatin.
116. Sometimes also pleasant dreams came over him.
117. Wî, dilgeş, kêfxweş û mesûd, xwe berdida nav pêlên xweş.
117. He, cheerful, joyful, and happy, let himself fall inside pleasant waves.
118. Lê xewnên vê koça dawîn ji yên kevn pir cihê ne.
118. But the dreams of this final migration are very different from the old ones.
119. Ew ne xweş in û ne jî xirab û xoftijî.
119. They are not pleasant and nor are they bad and terrifying.
120. Ew çawan in?
120. How are they?
121. Salixdan ne hêsan e.
121. To describe is not easy.
122. Bi kurtebirî, ew xewnên koça dawîn in.
122. In short, they are the dreams of the final migration.
123. Niha jî ew li deşteke fireh, bêser û ber e.
123. Now also he is on a wide, boundless plain.
124. Deşt di nav rengekî zer de ye.
124. The plain is inside a yellow color.
125. Aso û deşt bi hev re bûne yek.
125. The horizon and plain have become one together.
126. Deşt dibiriqe û carina leylan dide.
126. The plain shines and sometimes gives a mirage.
127. Di deştê de girên hûr hene.
127. In the plain are small hills.
128. Lê Memduh Selîm beg tênagihê ka ew çi gir in û ji çi hatine pê.
128. But Memduh Selim Beg does not understand what hills they are and from what they have come to exist.
129. Rengê giran, cih bi cih, diguherin.
129. The color of the hills, place by place, changes.
130. Gava ew reng diguherin, rengên nû, hêdî hêdî, bi ser yê kevn re tên û lê hukim dikin.
130. When those colors change, new colors, slowly slowly, come over the old one and rule over it.
131. Rengên giran weke rengên keskesorekê dixuyin.
131. The colors of the hills look like the colors of a rainbow.
132. Erdê deştê jî diguhere.
132. The ground of the plain also changes.
133. Carina ew dibe qûm, carina giya û hêşînahî, carina zevî, carina erdê qiraç.
133. Sometimes it becomes sand, sometimes grass and greenery, sometimes a field, sometimes barren land.
134. Ji dûr ve, li nik giran jî rawirên ecêb dixuyin.
134. From afar, near the hills also strange beasts appear.
135. Ew wan jî nas nake.
135. He does not recognize them either.
136. Rawir jî, weke tiştên din, diguherin.
136. The beasts also, like other things, change.
137. Ew carina dibin rawirên dirende û kerî bi kerî digerin û carina jî ew dibin rawirên fîrende û ref bi ref difirin.
137. They sometimes become predatory beasts and wander pack by pack, and sometimes also they become flying birds and fly flock by flock.

138. Di deştê de tu dar û av naxuyin.
138. In the plain no trees and water appear.
139. Di deştê de tiştê herî xweş dengê musikê ye.
139. In the plain the most pleasant thing is the sound of music.
140. Dengê musikeke têkel ji dûr ve, ji ew niqteyên ku aso û deşt bi hev re dibin yek, tê.
140. The sound of a mixed music comes from afar, from those points where the horizon and plain become one together.
141. Baş fahm dibe; deng dengê musikê ye.
141. It is well understood; the sound is the sound of music.
142. Lê kîjan musik?
142. But which music?
143. Ev yeka fahm nabe.
143. This thing is not understood.
144. Carina ew bi senfoniyeke babilîska 18-an ya Ewrûpayê dişibe, carina bi straneke gelêrî ya kurdî, carina bi soneteke xweş ya piyanoyê, carina bi musika klasîk ya erebî û carina jî bi şi'îreke farisî.
144. Sometimes it resembles a symphony of the 18th century whirlwind of Europe, sometimes a folk song of Kurdish, sometimes a pleasant sonata of piano, sometimes the classical music of Arabic, and sometimes a poem of Persian.
145. Guherînên deştê û musîkê li gor hev in.
145. The changes of the plain and the music are according to each other.
146. Ax, rengê hawirdor û rawir li gor musikê diguherin.
146. Ah, the color of the surroundings and the beasts change according to the music.
147. Lê belê, dengê musikê jî pir ji dûr tê.
147. But indeed, the sound of the music also comes from very far.
148. Yanê, di nav bêdengiyê de dengekî weke dengê musikê...
148. That is, inside the silence a sound like the sound of music...
149. «Memduh beg, xwe bilivîne, tiştekî bibêje, behsa rojên Wanê û Stembolê bike, ji kitêbên xwe tiştina bixwîne, bikene, bigirî, biqîre, behsa xwişka xwe bike, behsa rojên Anteqiyayê bike...
149. «Memduh Beg, move yourself, say something, speak of the days of Van and Istanbul, read something from your books, laugh, cry, scream, speak of your sister, speak of the days of Antakya...
150. Ji bo Xwedê tiştekî bibêje...»
150. For God's sake say something...»
151. Maliya wî, Wildan xanim, li kêleka wî rûniştiye, li rûyê wî yê kal dinihêre û dipeyive.
151. His wife, Wildan Xanim, sits at his side, looks at his old face, and speaks.
152. Çavên Memduh Selîm beg jî li wê dinihêrin û lêv jî dixwazin vebin û bikenin.
152. The eyes of Memduh Selim Beg also look at her, and the lips also want to open and laugh.
153. Lê nabe.
153. But it does not happen.
154. Bi tenê çavên vekirî û bi ken lê dinêrin.
154. Only the open and smiling eyes look at her.
155. «Mamo, mamo!
155. «Uncle, uncle!
156. Tu min dibihîsî?
156. Do you hear me?
157. Ez ji bajêr têm.
157. I come from the city.
158. Kurdên Şamê halê te dipirsin...
158. The Kurds of Damascus ask about your condition...
159. Îro dinya pir xweş e, tav germ e.
159. Today the world is very pleasant, the sun is warm.
160. Ez penceran vekim?»
160. Shall I open the windows?»
161. Memduh Selîm beg di koça xwe de pencereyek dibîne.
161. Memduh Selim Beg in his migration sees a window.
162. Pencereyeke pir stûr di navbera erd û asman de.
162. A very thick window between earth and sky.
163. Pencere hêdî hêdî vedibe.
163. The window slowly slowly opens.
164. Bi dû pencerê re deryake zelal û şîn dixuye.
164. Following the window a clear and blue sea appears.
165. Deryake stûr di navbera erd û asman de.
165. A thick sea between earth and sky.
166. Tîrêjên tavê li ser ava zelal diçirûsin.
166. The rays of the sun sparkle on the clear water.
167. Tu pêl li ser avê naxuyin.
167. No waves appear on the water.
168. Deng tune, her tişt di nav bêdengiyê de ye.
168. There is no sound, everything is in silence.
169. Ew li avê û tavê dinihêre.
169. He looks at the water and the sun.
170. Ew hem di nav avê de ye, hem jî li ser avê.
170. He is both inside the water and also on the water.
171. Lê ji nişkekê ve, av li ber wî diqelişe û jê coteke kevokên spî radibin û bi firê dikevin.
171. But suddenly, the water splits open before him and from it a pair of white pigeons rise and take flight.
172. Kevok weke pembû spî ne.
172. The pigeons are white like cotton.
173. Kevokên xweşik, çend car, li ser deryayê difirin û paşê jî, hêdî hêdî bi dûr dikevin û winda dibin.
173. Beautiful pigeons fly over the sea several times and then slowly drift away and disappear.
174. Bi dû kevokan re, av dîsan diqelişe û jê keçikeke tahzî radibe û bi firê dikeve.
174. Following the doves, the water breaks again and a beautiful girl rises and flies away.
175. Keçikeke tahzî, pir xweşik, pordirêj û bedew.
175. A young, very beautiful, long-haired and beautiful girl.
176. Keçik şil e û tîrêjên tavê li bedena wê ya spî dikevin û dilopên ku di bedena wê re diherikin, dibin weke lûlû û elmas.
176. The girl is wet, and the sun's rays fall on her white body, and the drops that flow down her body become like pearls and diamonds.
177. Serê memikên wê yên vekişiyayî dibiriqin.
177. Her protruding nipples glistened.
178. Bedena wê bi rengekî helesor diçirûse.
178. Her body glows in a horrible way.
179. Bejna keçikê carina dirêj dibe, carina jî weke bejna zarokekî, kin.
179. A girl's waist is sometimes long, sometimes short like a child's waist.
180. Keçik ber bi Memduh Selîm beg difîre û tê nêzîkî lê dike.
180. The girl flies towards Mamduh Selim Beg and approaches him.
181. Lê belê, tu carî ew xwe nagihîne wî.
181. However, he never reaches him.
182. Ew, çend car, li dor Memduh Selîm beg, ber bi jêr û jor, xwe ba dide.
182. He, several times, around Memduh Selim beg, moves up and down.
183. Lêvên wê jî dilizîn, lê Memduh Selîm beg dengê wî nabihîse.
183. Her lips are also burning, but Memduh Selim Beg doesn't hear his voice.
184. Paşê jî, keçik, rûyê wê ber bi wî, bi paşkî difire û winda dibe.
184. Then, the girl, her face towards him, flies backwards and disappears.
185. Bi dû windabûna keçikê re, derya jî winda dibe.
185. With the disappearance of the girl, the sea also disappears.
186. Naxêr, ew winda nabe, lê di derekî de xelas dibe.
186. No, it does not disappear, but it is saved in a way.
187. Dîsan pencereyeke stûr li ber Memduh Selîm beg vedibe.
187. Again, a thick window opens in front of Memduh Selim Beg.
188. Pencereyeke ewçend stûr ku erd û asman jê hatiye pê.
188. A window so thick that the earth and the sky are covered.

1031. Memduh Selim Beg does not write poetry, but reads it.
1032. Ew xwendevanekî dilsoz yê şi'îran e.
1032. He is a devoted reader of poetry.
1033. Li gor wî, dilê ku deriyê xwe ji şi'îr û germiya şi'îran re venake, dilekî nîvmirî ye.
1033. According to him, a heart that does not open its door to poetry and the warmth of poetry is a half-dead heart.
1034. Dilekî weke çoleke zuha, erdekî qiraç, deverekî bêbergeh û tahtekî hişk û zuha.
1034. A heart like a dry desert, a dry land, a barren place and a hard and dry throne.
1035. Li gor wî dil û şi'îr; yekitiya herî xweş, yekitiya zanîn û hîsan.
1035. According to him, heart and poetry; the most beautiful unity, the unity of knowledge and feelings.

1036. Mamduh Selim Beg is sitting in the Zfrahi garden and has opened the door of his heart to poetry.

1040. It's been a few days that a thin happiness, curtain by curtain, is coming to him.

1041. Memduh Selim Beg feels even younger now.

2756. Yanê du tayên pir ji hev cihê ew sermest kir.

2757. Since that day, the path of his life is like a path that goes through forests, rocks and valleys.
2758. Yanê riyekê ku di nav rengên têkel de ye.
2758. That is, a path in mixed colors.
2759. Ew niha li ser wê riyê ye û her dere.
2759. He is now on that path and everywhere.
2760. Ber bi hem amanc û hedefên rojane û hem jî yên dûr û dirêj.
2760. Towards both daily and long-term goals and objectives.
2761. Ber bi serfiraziyê, ber bi azadiyê, ber bi serketina dil.
2761. Towards success, towards freedom, towards the victory of the heart.
2762. Lê belê, li milê din, mij û dûmanê riya wî vegirtiye.
2762. However, on the other side, the fog and smoke blocked his way.
2763. Dar û daristan, çiya, zinar û şikeft li ber wî ne.
2763. Trees and forests, mountains, rocks and caves are before him.
2764. Ev rêwîtî dê li kû û çawan biqede?..
2764. Where and how will this journey end?
2765. Ma niha wexta pirs û gumanên weha ye!
2765. Is now the time for such questions and doubts!
2766. Rûyê ronî û çavên stûr lê dinihêrin.
2766. Bright face and thick eyes look at him.
2767. Germiyekê ku bi demeke dirêj jê bi dûr bû, bi ser wî re tê.
2767. A warmth that was far from him for a long time comes over him.
2768. Ew dipeyive, tiştina dibêje.
2768. He speaks, says something.
2769. Lê peyvên wî ewçend bi best in ku wekî ku ew ji kûrahiya dil tên.
2769. But his words are so good that they come from the heart.
2770. Peyvên wî wekî kahniyeke boş, germ û zelal diherikin.
2770. His words flow like an empty priest, warm and clear.
2771. Rûyê ronî bîhnvedanek, ferrehiyek, rehetiyek, sermestiyeke xweş bi ser wî de tîne û beden û zîhnê wî bi vê yekê vedije, zînde dibe.
2771. The bright face brings a fragrance, a spaciousness, a comfort, a pleasant headiness to him and his body and mind revives with this.
2772. Ev çavên li hember, ev rû û bedena li hember dilê wî vedigire.
2772. This eyes against, this face and body against his heart.
2773. Belê, êdî baş dixuye, êdî eşkere ye;Xezalali hember rûniştî pê li deriyê dilê Memduh Selîm Begê dike.
2773. Well, now it sounds good, now it's clear; Khazalali is kicking the door of Mamduh Selim Beg's heart.
2774. Ew dê bibe stûna mala wî.

2822. (Ew hem ji dengê bilûrê û hem jîji dengê kemançê, hem ji dastaneke kevnar û hem ji romaneke nûjen, hem ji stranên dengbêjekî û hem ji resîtalên oparetekê hez dike.

2823. Lê ew bi xêra kitêb û tecruban ferqên wan jî dizane.) Ew ji kitêban hîn bûbû ku meriv, li her derê cîhanê, çi bigire eynî tiştî dijîn û hîs dikin, lê bi kincine cihê yên netewî û herêmî.

2824. Thanks to the books, he realized that the stories of the Greeks, the Aztecs and the Ancans, the Chinese and the Japanese, the Reds and the Blacks, and the Kurds are the same.

His eventful life; a sweet childhood in Bedlis, in the old neighborhood of Eli Koli, a young man with a left hand, studying and studying in Istanbul, the years of the "Harbiyeh" military school in Istanbul, working with the Kurds and Kurdish organizations, hoping for unity and freedom, a leader and officer, a commander in the world war, the commander of the Ottoman troops in the city of Agiri Bayzid, the beginning of his friendship with the Agiri mountain, against the soldiers of the army Fighting the Russian emperor, working against the Turkish policy after the establishment of the Republic of Turkey, one of the founders of the Kurdish organization, the Kurdistan Independence Committee, in 1924, together with his friends, rebelled against the Turkish state, defeated and escaped, a member of Khoybuun, the military leader of Khoybuun and Agiri.

4674. a- Qomandarê giştî yê jandermeriya Agriyê Temir Axa, bi hêzên ku li bin destê wî datînin li bervarê 3 juiye 1930, bi arîkariya xêlê xwe şemkan ku li malbenda Qolpê rûdinin, êrîş dide ser navenda qezaya Qolpê, paş dagirkirina bajêr pêşmergeyan heya girtina gundê Pernavot berepêş bişîne.

5518. Wexta malkambax niha her tişt guhertiye; reng bi tenê bûne rengên bed û mirdar, bîhn bi tenê bûne bîhnên genî, tahm bi tenê bûne tahmên tahl, tûj û tirş, deng bi tenê bûne dengên nexweş û hîs bi tenê bûne hîsên mirî...
5518. Homecoming time has changed everything now; colors became only ugly and dead colors, smells became only genial smells, tastes became only bitter, sharp and sour tastes, sounds became only sick sounds and feelings became only dead feelings...

5525. Wî di destpêka 1900 an de kitêbeke H.A.Giles xwendibû; ChuangTzu.
5525. He had read a book by H.A. Giles in the beginning of 1900; ChuangTzu.
5526. Di kitêbê de, berî 2500 salan Chuang Tzu xewnek dibîne.
5526. In the book, 2500 years ago, Chuang Tzu had a dream.
5527. Di xewnê de ew pepûlekeke biçûk e û difire.
5527. In the dream, he is a small butterfly and flies.
5528. Gava ew ji xew hişyar dibe, ew nizane ka ew pepûlek e ku di xewna xwe de merivekî dîtibû yan jî, ji bervajiyê, ew merivekî bû ku di xewna xwe de pepûlekek dîtibû.
5528. When he wakes up, he doesn't know if he is a ghost who saw a man in his dream or, on the contrary, it was a man who saw a ghost in his dream.
5529. Chuang Tzu weha digot; «Min di xewna xwe de didît ku ez pepûleyek bûm ku li asmanan difiriyam û min tu tişt di derheqê Chuang Tzu de nizanîbû.»
5529. Chuang Tzu said: "I dreamed that I was a pigeon flying in the sky and I knew nothing about Chuang Tzu."
5530. Chuang Tzu hosteyê xewnan bû.
5530. Chuang Tzu was a master of dreams.
5531. Bê guman.
5531. Of course.
5532. Wî wext li gor xwe eyar dikir.

5533. Ew serdestê wextê bû.
5533. He was the master of time.
5534. Reng, bîhn, tahm, deng û hîs li gor daxwaza wî şekil digirtin.

5535. Ew hosteyê peyv, gotin, qise û terman bû jî.
5535. He was also a master of words, sayings, stories and terms.
5536. Wî bi xwe naverokek dida wan.
5536. He himself gave them content.
5537. Gava wî dixwest, ew dibû pepûle û gava dixwest jî, ew dibû meriv.
5537. When he wanted, he became a people and when he wanted, he became a man.
5538. Memduh Selîm Beg jî divê bibe serdestê wextê.
5538. Memduh Selim Beg should also be the master of time.
5539. Wext divê li gor daxwaza wî şekil bigire, ne ku ew.
5539. Time should take shape according to his will, not him.
5540. Gava bîhn lê teng dibe, nefes lê diçike, ew divê bibe pepûleyek û bi firê bikeve.
5540. When the smell is tight, the breath is short, it should turn into a lump and fly away.

5652. 1933 is also the decade of the founding of the Republic of Turkey.

5653. When the Republic of Turkey was established, Memduh Selim Beg also left Turkey...

5658. Three weeks ago, on the 21st of the 12th month of 1932, the Turkish ambassador saw Memduh Selim Beg.

5660. The reason for meeting was this; if Memduh Selim Beg returns to Turkey, he will be pardoned and able to live freely as a citizen of Turkey.

5836. Her heart is burning with Memduh Selim Beg.
5837. Ew dixwaze alîkariyê bike.
5837. He wants to help.
5838. Lê çawan?

5839. She went and saw Feriha, talked to her, was very happy and wanted to win her heart, to please her.
5840. Lê nebû.
5840. But it didn't happen.
5841. «Mallesef, Ferîha pir li dûr e.

5842. If he were close to us, we would, little by little, convince him...

5844. He may change in the coming days."
5845. Gotinên Rûşen Xanimê.

5846. Jê re.

5850. As in most cases, the issue is again the love of Memduh Selim Beg and Feriha.
5851. Sal dibuhurin, lê mesele, pirs û birîn her wekî xwe dimînin.

5852. Çima?
5852. Why?

5853. Why was that?

5854. Mrs. Ruşen asked Feriha something that everyone is thinking about: why did she marry an old man who had two wives?
5855. Bersîva wê di gotinên wê de ye.
5855. The answer is in her words.
5856. «Ez ji kekê Memduh re nebûm yar, lê ez ji kesekî din re jî nebûm...»
5856. "I didn't like Memduh's cake, but I didn't like anyone else either..."
5857. «Ax Memduh Beg, ne tu û ne jî mêrên kurd, hûn kes ji halê jinan fahm nakin.
5857. "Ah Memduh Beg, neither you nor the Kurdish men, you do not understand the situation of women.
5858. Qet hûn nizanin, tênagihên ew çi difikirin, çi hîs dikin...
5858. You never know what they think, what they feel...

5859. Do you know, Memduh Beg, where did Feriha get this idea from?"

5863. Ew ji Binevşa Narînê hîn bûye ku xwe bi saxî biçîne axa reş.»
5863. He learned from Binevşa Narîn to plant himself alive in the black land.
5864. Binevşa Narîn...
5864. Binevsha Narin...

5865. Binevsha Narin and Jebeliye Hekkar.

5866. Dastana kevn, dastana evînê.
5866. The old epic, the epic of love.

5867. Yes, in those beautiful days, when Memduh Selim Beg was getting to know his Khazala's body under the shadow of love, he had also told her about Binevsha Narin.

5868. He wanted Feriha to learn that story.
5869. Evîna Binevşa Narînê, evîna keça koçeran.
5869. Binevsha Narin's love, the love of a nomad's daughter.
5870. Evîna serokeşîrê çiyayên Hekkarê.
5870. The love of the chief priest of Hekkar mountains.
5871. Evîneke xweş, bi kul û birîn, kevnare.
5871. A good, old-fashioned love affair.
5872. «Delorî Cembeliyê min delorî, emrê min bi heyran, serê min bi gorî!..»
5872. "Delori Jambeliyeh, my delight, my command with admiration, my head in accordance!.."

5874. Who knew that these words of Binevsh would become hadith and enter Feriha's mouth.
5875. «Bila mêrê meriya bi dilê meriya bî, bila nan hebîû dew tune bî, bila xwarina meriya garisê bi gilgil bî; bila lehêfa meriya ezmanê bilind bî; bila doşega meriya ji erdê şil bî; bila belîfa meriya ji kevir bî; bila tûrê parsê tim li mil bî; bila binê tûrê meriya bi qul bî; bila cihê meriya ne li vir bî, li sînorê Ecem û gêwir bî; bila mêrê meriya ne bi dilê meriya bî, bila sibê heya êvarê ne kar bî, ne şixul bî, xwarin û libas pir bî; dilê meriya tim bi kul bî...»
5875. "Let the husband of the mary be with the heart of the mary, let there be bread and no dew, let the food of the mary of the garis be gilgil; may the glory of heaven be high; let the mat be wet from the ground; let the bed of Mary be made of stone; let the beggar's net always be at hand; let the bottom of the net be perforated; let the place of death be not here, but be at the border of Ecem and Gewir; may the husband of Mary be not to Mary's heart, may you not be busy from morning to evening, may you have plenty of food and clothes; May your heart always be happy..."
5876. Jiyan dubare dibe.
5876. Life repeats itself.
5877. Derd û keserên dastanan îroj jîbi car dibin.
5877. The problems and characters of the epics are still common today.

5879. Jiyana nenas, jiyana piralî!..
5879. Unknown life, multifaceted life!..

5880. 12 Berbanga Antaqiyayê.
5880. 12 Dawn of Antioch.
5881. Li aliyê Rojhelat, di nav çiyayên hêşîn û berz de tav hiltê.
5881. In the East, the sun rises between the green and high mountains.
5882. Giran, giran.
5882. Heavy, heavy.
5883. Li aliyê rojava, tîrêjên jar yên tavê pêlên deryayê hembêz dikin û li ser diçirûsin.
5883. In the west, the sun's rays hug the sea waves and sparkle on them.
5884. Tariya şevê winda dibe.
5884. The darkness of the night disappears.
5885. Yek-du stêrkên mayî jî koç dikin û derin.
5885. The remaining one or two stars migrate and leave.
5886. Wext reng diguherîne.
5886. Time changes color.
5887. Rengeke ronî, hêdî hêdî, hawirdor vedigire.
5887. A bright, slow, ambient color.
5888. Di nav bêdengiyeke zîz de.
5888. In a deep silence.
5889. Ji dengê pêlên avê pê ve, tu deng tune.
5889. There is no sound except for the sound of water waves.
5890. Pêl jî, hêdî hêdî, xwe radigihînin qeraxê.
5890. The waves, slowly, reach the shore.

5891. The waves are in a sweet game; the world wakes up and they laugh and sing.
5892. Bi awayê xwe, bi zimanê xwe.
5892. In his own way, in his own language.
5893. Li qeraxa avê jî Memduh Selîm Beg.
5893. Memduh Selim Beg at the water's edge.
5894. Ew ji rengguherîna tebîyatê hez dike.
5894. He likes to change the color of health.
5895. Di demên weha xweş, bêdeng û balkêş de ew xwe zînde û jiyayî hîs dike.
5895. In such beautiful, quiet and interesting moments he feels alive and alive.
5896. Gava rengên ronî hawirdor vedigirin, ronahiyekê di nava wî de jî hiltê.
5896. When bright colors cover the environment, a light rises in him as well.
5897. Hingê bedena wî germ dibe û dilê wî bi germiyeke taybetî hildavê.
5897. Then his body warms up and his heart rises with a special warmth.
5898. Digel her celeb derd, kul û keserî...
5898. With all kinds of pain, suffering and suffering...
5899. Niha, ew, dîsan, li ser riya biryarên girîng e.

5900. Now, he needs a new move again.
5901. Mixabin.
5901. I am sorry.

5904. Isal, yanê 1937, qedera Antaqiyayê diyar dike.
5904. This year, 1937, determines the fate of Antioch.
5905. Turkiye doza Antaqiya, Iskenderûn û Kirikxanê dike.
5905. Turkey claims Antioch, Iskenderun and Kirikkhan.
5906. Piştî têkçûna dewleta Osmanî, ev dever, herwekî Lubnan û Sûriyê, ji aliyê Franseyê dihat îdare kirin.
5906. After the defeat of the Ottoman state, this area, like Lebanon and Syria, was administered by France.
5907. Niha, 17 sal bi dû peymana Lozanê re, Turkiye ji Fransê daxwaz dike ku ev dever bibin deverên Turkiyê.
5907. Now, 17 years after the Lausanne Treaty, Turkey is asking France to make these areas part of Turkey.
5908. Par Fransê azadiya Sûriyê qebûl kir.
5908. Last year, France accepted the freedom of Syria.
5909. U serokatiya nû ya Sûriyê jî dixwaze ev dever di nav tixûbên Sûriyê de bimînin û dawe dike ku ev dever ereb in.
5909. And the new leadership of Syria wants these areas to remain within the boundaries of Syria and says that these areas are Arab.
5910. Franse?
5910. French?
5911. Franse jî, wekî her carî, carina li ba tirkan, carina jî li ba ereban e.
5911. France, as always, is sometimes with the Turks and sometimes with the Arabs.
5912. Ew carina dixwaze ev dever xweser bin, carina bibin tirk û carina jî bibin ereb.
5912. Sometimes he wants these areas to be autonomous, sometimes to become Turks and sometimes to become Arabs.
5913. Lê serokamîrê van deveran General CoUet(belê, ew bûye general) bi ser tirkan e.
5913. But the leader of these areas is General CoUet (yes, he has become a general) over the Turks.
5914. Ew wekî tirkekî dixebite da ku ev dever tevî tixûbên Tirkiyê bin.
5914. He works as a Turk so that these areas are within the borders of Turkey.
5915. Yanê bi gotineke din, rewş baş naxuyê.
5915. In other words, the situation does not look good.
5916. Memduh Selîm Beg ji tecrubên xwe, ji tecrubên tarîxa gelê xwe dizane; welatên bêkes, bêpişt, bêhêz nikarin xwe li hember hêz û welatên stûrtir ragirin.

5917. Ew dibin para şûrê Ruhistîn.
5917. They become part of the sword of Ruhistin.
5918. Ew masiyên biçûk in û di şerê masiyan de ew dibin para masiyên mezin...
5918. They are small fish and in the fish fight they become part of the big fish...

6217. U tiştekî din; Memduh Selîm Beg hê jî xebata xwe ya siyasî didomîne.
6217. And something else; Memduh Selim Beg still continues his political work.
6218. Hê jî peywendiyên wî yên siyasî hene.
6218. He still has political connections.
6219. Lê bê guman, ew hêvî, şewk û heyecana 1920-30 an nemaye.
6219. But of course, the hope, sparkle and excitement of the 1920-30s is gone.
6220. Ji wan rojan tiştê ku ew pir meraq dike, kite-kitên şoreşa Agirî û serpêhatiyên Ihsan Nûrî Paşa ne.
6220. From those days, what he is most interested in are the stories of the Agiri revolution and the adventures of Ihsan Nuri Pasha.
6221. Şoreş têkçû.
6221. The revolution failed.
6222. Ihsan Nûrî Paşa û pîreka wî xwe spartin bextê Iranê û ew niha li Tehranê dijîn.
6222. Ihsan Nuri Pasha and his old lady relied on the luck of Iran and they now live in Tehran.
6223. Lê belê, Memduh Selîm Begê tu carî keys nedît ku bûyerên têkçûnê û rewşa Ihsan Nûrî û xanima wî bizanibe.
6223. However, Memduh Selim Beg never had the chance to know the events of the defeat and the condition of Ihsan Nuri and his wife.
6224. Wî û Ihsan Nûrî Paşa, ji wê rojê pê ve, tu caran hevûdu nedîtin.
6224. He and Ihsan Nuri Pasha never saw each other after that day.
6225. Ew wan meraq dike.
6225. It makes them wonder.
6226. Ferîha venegerî.
6226. Feriha did not return.
6227. Ew hê jî li Urdinê ye.
6227. He is still in Jordan.
6228. Birîna Memduh Selîm Begê sax nebû.
6228. Memduh Selim Beg's wound did not heal.
6229. Ew her diêşe.
6229. It always hurts.
6230. Ew hê jî li hêviya hatina Ferîha'yê ye.
6230. He is still waiting for Feriha's arrival.
6231. Memduh Selîm Begê ku tu carî nedixwest bi tenê bijî, hê jî, tenê dijî.
6231. Memduh Selim Beg, who never wanted to live alone, still lives alone.
6232. Memduh Selîm Begê ku mal, jin û zarok dil dikir, di vê payiza umirê xwe de jî, bi tenê xwediyê kitêban e.
6232. Memduh Selim Beg, who loved home, wife and children, even in this autumn of his age, is the only owner of books.
6233. Kitêb bûn zarokên wî.
6233. Books became his children.
6234. Ew her xebitî ku dinya bibe dinyayeke çêtir.
6234. He always worked to make the world a better world.
6235. Wî xwe westan ku jiyan hîn çêtir be.
6235. He tried to make life better.
6236. Lê niha, di payiza umirê xwe de, ew pê dihese ku jiyana wî bi xwe dere.
6236. But now, in the fall of his age, he realizes that his life is on its own.
6237. Wî xwend, pir xwend.
6237. He read, read a lot.
6238. Wî dil kir ku pir tişt hîn be, pir tişt bizanibe.
6238. He wanted to learn a lot, to know a lot.
6239. Ew bi klasîkên kurdî, rojhelat û roja vayê mezin bû.
6239. He grew up with Kurdish classics, Rojhelat and Rojvay.
6240. Di salên zanîngehê de jî, wî nivîskar û feylesofên nûjen xwendin.
6240. Even during his university years, he studied modern writers and philosophers.
6241. Ew bû hevalbendê kitabxanan.
6241. He became a friend of libraries.
6242. Li Parîsê, li odeyeke pir biçûk û sar, di bin ronahiya çirayeke jar de, wî çand û edebiyata fransizî hîn çêtir nasî, şoreş û medeniyeta Fransê hîn çêtir hîn bû.
6242. In Paris, in a very small and cold room, under the light of a jar lamp, he got to know the French culture and literature even better, he learned the French revolution and civilization even better.
6243. Kitab, kovar û rojname li ber serê wî riziyan.
6243. Books, magazines and newspapers rotted in front of him.
6244. Li Galatayê, di nav dengên qahpik û serxweşan de, wî serê xwe bi siyasetê û teoriyên siyasetê êşand.
6244. In Galata, among the voices of drunkards and drunkards, he hurt his head with politics and political theories.
6245. Li Antaqiyayê, cihê ku bîhna wî lê derdiket, kitabxana wî bû.
6245. In Antakya, the place where his smell came from, was his library.
6246. Wî nedixwar, kitab dikirîn.
6246. He didn't eat, he bought books.
6247. Wî venedixwar kovar dikirîn.
6247. He didn't buy magazines.
6248. Wî li xwe nedikir, rojname dikirîn.
6248. He didn't wear it, he bought newspapers.
6249. Ew li ser riya zanînê bû derwêş, bû dîn.
6249. He became a dervish, a madman on the path of knowledge.
6250. Lê mixabin, hezar mixabin...
6250. But alas, a thousand alas...
6251. Ev xîret, zanîn û ked ji derdê evînê re nebûn çare.
6251. This diligence, knowledge and hard work did not solve the pain of love.
6252. Digel evçend zanînê, wî dermana birîna evînê nedît.
6252. Despite all this knowledge, he did not find the cure for love's wound.
6253. Niha jî, ew li kitabxana xwe rûniştiye û van tiştan dinivîse.
6253. Even now, he is sitting in his library and writing these things.
6254. Wekî nameyekê.
6254. Like a letter.
6255. Ji dostê xwe yê gorbehîşt Celader Bedirxan re.
6255. To my dear friend Celader Bedirkhan.
6256. Belê, ji Celadet Bedirxan re.
6256. Yes, to Celadet Bedirkhan.
6257. Memduh Selîm Beg her hefte ji sê kesan re name dinivîse.
6257. Memduh Selim Beg writes letters to three people every week.
6258. Ji sê kesên mirî re; bavê wî, Celadet AlîBedirxan û Ferîha.
6258. To the three dead people; his father, Celadet AliBadirkhan and Feriha.
6259. Roja sêşemê, piştî nîvro ji bavê xwe re.
6259. On Tuesday, in the afternoon to his father.
6260. Roja çarşemê, piştî nîvro ji Celadet Alî Bedirxan re.
6260. On Wednesday, afternoon to Celadet Ali Bedirkhan.
6261. Roja pêncşemê, piştî nîvro jî ji Ferîha'yê re.
6261. On Thursday, in the afternoon, to Feriha.
6262. Gerçî Ferîha nemiriye.
6262. Although Feriha is not dead.
6263. Gerçî Memduh Selîm Begê hê jî hêvî heye ku Ferîha dê vegere.
6263. Although Memduh Selim Beg still has hope that Feriha will return.
6264. Lê bi alîkariya nameyan, ew pê re dipeyive, wê bi bîr tîne.
6264. But with the help of letters, he talks to her, remembers her.
6265. Mixabin ku Memduh Selîm Beg ne nivîskar e.
6265. Unfortunately, Memduh Selim Beg is not a writer.
6266. Eger wî bikaribûya, wî dê romanekê li ser evînê binivîsa.
6266. If he could, he would write a novel about love.
6267. Romanek ku bi kêfxweşî û serfirazî diqede, evîndar digihên mirazên xwe û dibin mesûd.
6267. A novel that ends with happiness and success, the lovers reach their goals and become happy.
6268. Lê ew nikare tu romanan binivîse.
6268. But he cannot write any novels.
6269. Di dewsa romanan de ew name dinivîse.
6269. Instead of novels, he writes letters.
6270. Bi vî awayî, ew bi xwe re û bi qedirgirên xwe re dipeyive.
6270. In this way, he speaks to himself and to his admirers.

6271. «Belê, mîrê min...
6271. "Yes, my lord...
6272. evîn û sewda dînîtiya herî mezin e.
6272. love and affection is the greatest religion.
6273. Lê dînîtiyeke welê ku meriv bê wê jî nabe...
6273. But it's a good obsession that you can't live without...
6274. Mîrê min, ez jî li rê me, ber bi te têm.
6274. My lord, I am also on the way, coming towards you.
6275. Di demeke kurt de, ez li nik te me.
6275. In a short time, I will be with you.
6276. Li hêviya min be...»
6276. Expect me..."

6277. 4 Destpêka 1965 an.

6279. It's raining outside.

6282. Ew bi ken e.
6282. He is smiling.

6299. Ez bi xwe jî baş bi vê yekê nizanim, lê li gor gotinan, ew ji peyva araqî ya erebî tê.
6299. I don't know about it myself, but according to the sayings, it comes from the Arabic word for alcohol.
6300. Yanê xwîdan.
6300. They eat it.

6301. That is, the drink that makes you sweat.

6302. The beautiful and sweet grape changes color, falls into the glass, changes color with water in the glass, becomes white and burns our gray.
6303. Gewrî ewçend dişewite ku meriv xwîdan dide...»
6303. The gray burns so much that one sweats..."
6304. Araq, vexwarina araqê, rewşa kurdan, nezanî, dijîtîû berberî, hukimeta nû ya ereb li Sûriyê, hal û hewala dost û hevalan, rewş li Turkiyê û li Kurdistana Iraqê û hwd...
6304. Vodka, drinking vodka, the situation of the Kurds, ignorance, poverty, the new Arab government in Syria, the situation of friends and colleagues, the situation in Turkey and Iraqi Kurdistan, etc.
6305. Tiştên ku di şeveke weha de tên peyivîn, pir in.
6305. There are many things that are discussed in such a night.

6311. Xanimên pak û delal pir in.
6311. There are many pure and lovely ladies.
6312. Tu divê bi yekîre bizewicî...»
6312. You should marry someone..."
6313. Memduh Selîm Beg çi bibêje?

6318. The neighborhood of Muhajirin was the neighborhood of the autumn of his life and also his last neighborhood in life.

6325. I have overcome most of these things and left them behind.

6327. Ne zewac...

6328. Em çawan bikin!
6328. How do we do it!
6329. Qedera min jî weha bû.

6330. Eger yek ji ew nameyên ku min ji Agiriyê şandibûn, bigihîşta cih, niha ez jî zewicî û xwediyê zar û zêç bûm.
6330. If one of the letters I sent from Agiri reached the destination, now I would be married and have children.
6331. Eger hevalekî ji we xwe bigîhanda çiyê, eger rê li min nehata girtin, eger Ferîha û dê û bavê wê nelezandina, eger edet û toran çavên Ferîha'yê kor nekirina, dîsan, ez niha zewicî bûm Lê nebû...
6331. If one of your friends had reached the mountain, if my path had not been blocked, if Feriha and her parents had not hurried, if customs and nets had not blinded Feriha's eyes, again, I would be married now. But it didn't happen...
6332. Em çawan bikin?»
6332. How do we do it?"
6333. Xwezî «eger»ên ku ew behs dike, bihatina cih.

6334. Xwezî her roja wî bi evînê bihata neqişandin.
6334. I wish his every day was filled with love.
6335. Xwezî daxwaz û mirazên wî nequrmiçîna û jiyana wî bibûya bergeheke rengîn.
6335. I wish that his desires and wishes would not be destroyed and that his life would be a colorful one.
6336. Lê ew niha, di payiza umirê xwe de, baş dizane ku jiyan ne bergeheke rengîn e û ne jî şênahiyeke bêdawîn e.
6336. But now, in the fall of his age, he knows very well that life is not a colorful place, nor is it an endless life.

6337. He knows that there are always pitfalls against the life of the old age...
6338. heye ku di ser de jî, jiyan bi xwe bûye kemîn.

6339. Unfortunately, after so much speed, running, work and hard work for many years, that trap is acceptable.

6976. The boys also rush to him.
6977. Lê piştî bîskekê, ew dîsan dest pê dike û nefes digire.
6977. But after a while, he starts breathing again.
6978. Hêdî hêdî.
6978. Slowly.
6979. Kesên doralî li hev dinihêrin û dibişirin.
6979. People around look at each other and smile.
6980. Lê piştî çend nefesên pêşîn yên baş, dîsan, bîhn lê diçike.
6980. But after the first few good breaths, again, the smell hits him.
6981. Ew dixwaze pihêt, pir pihêt nefes bigire û bide.
6981. He wants to inhale and exhale deeply, deeply.
6982. Sînga wî radibe û dadike.
6982. His chest rises and falls.
6983. Ev yeka, bi qasî çend saniyan, dewam dike, lê paşê, dîsan, ew giran dibe û nefes lê tê birîn.
6983. This lasts for a few seconds, but then, again, he becomes heavy and short of breath.
6984. «Çû rehmetê, mala minê, çû rehmetê!..»
6984. "Gone to mercy, my house, gone to mercy!"

6985. Lê na, Memduh Selîm Beg, dîsan, dest bi nefesgirtinê dike.
6985. But no, Memduh Selim Beg starts breathing again.
6986. Icar hîn çêtir û bi dûzan.
6986. Now even better and with more.
6987. Lêvên wî vedibin.
6987. His lips open.
6988. Lêv hêdî hêdî dihezin.
6988. The lips move slowly.
6989. Ew dil dike tiştekî bibêje.
6989. He wants to say something.
6990. Lê nabe.
6990. But it doesn't happen.
6991. Li eniya wî dilopên xwîdanê civiyane.
6991. Drops of blood gathered on his forehead.
6992. Wîldan Xanim bi destmaleke spî eniya wî paqij dike.
6992. Mrs. Wildan wipes his forehead with a white handkerchief.
6993. «Bibêje, bipeyive Memduh Beg...
6993. "Speak, speak Memduh Beg...
6994. xîret bike, tiştekî bibêje...»
6994. try hard, say something..."
6995. Çavên Memduh Selîm Begê wekî ku ne yên wî bin.
6995. Memduh Salim Beg's eyes are as if they are not his own.
6996. Wekî ku kesekî coteke çav danîbin ser kortika çavan.
6996. As if someone placed a pair of eyes on the eye cortex.
6997. Ew ewçend vekirî û bêhereket in.
6997. They are so open and unmoved.
6998. Bi tenê ew li bana odê dinihêrin.
6998. They just look at the ceiling of the room.
6999. Nêrîneke sabît û sakîn.
6999. A fixed and calm look.
7000. U westiyayî.
7000. You are tired.
7001. Pir westiyayî.
7001. Very tired.
7002. Lê belê, ew di koça xwe de, di nav pêlên ava spî de masiyeke stûr dibîne.
7002. However, he finds a thick fish in the waves of white water in his migration.
7003. Masiyeke stûr û zerik.
7003. A thick and yellow fish.
7004. Masî li dor wî dere û tê.
7004. The fish come and go around him.
7005. Masî pir xweşik e, pûlên bedena wê dibiriqin.
7005. The fish is very beautiful, the scales of its body are shining.
7006. Memduh Selîm Beg jê dernaxe ka ew çi celeb masî ye.
7006. Memduh Selim Beg does not say what kind of fish it is.
7007. Lê wî tu carîmasiyeke evçend xweşik nedîtîye.
7007. But he has never seen such a beautiful fish.
7008. Lê tiştê ecêb, masîjî şekil û reng diguherîne.
7008. But the amazing thing is, massage changes shape and color.
7009. Gava ew nêzîkî li Memduh Selîm Begê dike, ew masî ye, lê gava ew jê bi dûr dikeve, ew dibe keçikek.
7009. When he approaches Mamduh Selim Beg, he is a fish, but when he moves away from him, he turns into a girl.
7010. Keçikeke bedew, pordirêj û bedenxweş.
7010. A beautiful, long haired and fit girl.
7011. Keçik jî dibiriqe.
7011. The girl is also shining.
7012. Memduh Selîm Beg kêfxweş e.
7012. Memduh Selim Beg is happy.
7013. Ne bi tenê kêfxweş, ew sermest e jî.
7013. It's not just fun, it's fun too.
7014. Ne bi tenê sermest, serxweş e jî.
7014. He is not only drunk, he is also drunk.
7015. Digel ku ava spî nefes lê diçikîne, ew xwe ranagire û carina devê xwe vedike û ava spî vedixwe.
7015. While breathing in the white water, he does not hold back and sometimes opens his mouth and drinks the white water.
7016. Masî li pêş, ew li paş, bi hev re, di nav pêlên spî de, ew derin.
7016. The fish in the front, he in the back, together, in the white waves, they enter.
7017. Masî rêberî lê dike.
7017. The fish guides him.
7018. Bi qasî demekê, ew bi hev re derin.
7018. For a while, they went together.
7019. Paşê, ji nişka ve, deriyek li ber wan dixuye.
7019. Then, suddenly, a door opens in front of them.
7020. Deriyekî pir stûr û neqişkirî, wekî deriyê keleheke stûr.
7020. A very thick and carved door, like the door of a thick castle.
7021. Her du milên derî, hêdî hêdî, li ber wan vedibin.
7021. Both sides of the door slowly open in front of them.
7022. Masî li pêşî, ew li paşî, ew ber bi derî derin.
7022. Fish in the front, he in the back, he goes to the door.
7023. Lê berî ku ew bigihên derî, Memduh Selîm Beg, dîsan, bi kêfxweşî, devê xwe vedike.
7023. But before they reach the door, Memduh Selim Beg, happily, opens his mouth again.

7024. "Wolf, Wolf...
7025. Memduh Beg dere!..»
7025. Memduh Beg dere!..”

7026. Rûyê Memduh Selîm Begê diguhere.

7027. His face is red as hell.

7029. Tiştê ku meriv bike, nemaye.
7029. There is nothing left to do.
7030. Her tişt êdî bêkêr e.
7030. Everything is useless now.
7031. Memduh Selîm Beg koç dike, dere.
7031. Memduh Selim Beg is moving.

7032. His mouth, strangely, retracts.
7033. Ew dixwaze nefes bigire, lê nefes lê tê birîn.
7033. He wants to breathe, but his breath is cut off.
7034. Çavên wî niha hîn bêtir vekirî ne.
7034. His eyes are now even more open.
7035. Ji devê wî tu peyv dernakeve, digel ku ew dil dike.
7035. No words come out of his mouth, even though he is heartbroken.
7036. Edî qefesa sîngê jî ranabe.
7036. The chest does not even rise.
7037. U xire xir pê dikeve.
7037. He is crying.
7038. Xire xir dewsa nefesê digire.
7038. Snoring takes the place of breathing.
7039. Xire xireke nerm.
7039. Wear a soft cloth.
7040. Wekî ku ew, merivê nerm û ziravbihîstiyar lawan bike û xatir bixwaze.
7040. As he, the gentle and sensitive man bows and says goodbye.
7041. Bi dû xire xirê re jî bêdengiya ebedî.
7041. Eternal silence followed by silence.

7053. 113 46 Stockholm Sweden Mehmed Uzun, 1953, is from North Kurdistan.
7054. Piştî cunta eskerî li Tirkiyê, 1970, ew hat girtin.
7054. After the military junta in Turkey, 1970, he was arrested.
7055. Bi qasî du salan, ew li girtîxanên Diyarbekir û Ankarê ma.
7055. For about two years, he was imprisoned in Diyarbakir and Ankara.
7056. Di sala 1976 an de, gava kovara Rizgarî dest bi weşînê kir, Mehmed Uzun bû berpisiyarê kovarê.
7056. In 1976, when Rizgari magazine started publishing, Mehmed Uzun became the editor of the magazine.
7057. Ji ber vê yekê jî ew hat girtin û 8 meh li girtixanê Ankarê ma.
7057. That's why he was arrested and spent 8 months in Ankara prison.

7059. In Sweden, he was in charge of the magazine Rizgariya Kurdistan, 1979-81.
